 He was born on 29 November 1913 in Balrampur in Gonda district of Uttar Pradesh

 Under his influence, Sardar read Vladimir Ilyich Ulyanov Lenin and Karl Heinrich Marx

 The combination of the capable and the best of the times, led to the rise of Ali Sardar Jafri as a poet whose poetry was a reflection of the pain and suffering of the toiling masses

 deshbhar main faili hui hajaaron-hajaar kilometre lambii rail patariyon ko automatic tareeke se jaanch-parakh paane ke liye bhartiya railway is samay dakshin africa ke ultrasonic broken rail ditection system trial kar rahi he
 Trial-ultrasonic broken rail detection system is a technology developed by the South African Department of Defense in which the fracture of rail tracks can be detected in time using ultrasonic waves
 is takanic kaa pareekshan is samay uttar railway main muradabad-saharanpur rail section par rudki stesan or hindon cabin ke bich main kiya ja rahaa he

 '' desh kii sheersh adaalat ne dilli hoicourt ke faisle ko barkaraar rakhaa ki mahilaayein or peedit 2005 ke gharelu hinsa kanoon main mahila sangrakshan ke praavdhaanon kaa upyog kar sakati he, bhale hi kathith hinsa kanoon lagu hone ke pehle hui ho
